  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1773ebd1-73bb-45c8-b680-b75dee9efefc'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer5670049246308057716">Jet McAlister has a secret. Eddie Chavez has the hots for Jet (not to mention Eddie’s just plain hot). Jet has too many problems to realize that Eddie’s interested. Eddie loses patience when Jet ends her waitressing shift at a strip club with a knife at her throat.   <span id="freeText5670049246308057716" style="display:none">Jet McAlister has a secret. Eddie Chavez has the hots for Jet (not to mention Eddie’s just plain hot). Jet has too many problems to realize that Eddie’s interested. Eddie loses patience when Jet ends her waitressing shift at a strip club with a knife at her throat. Since Eddie’s a cop, he figures he can help. Since Jet’s used to solving everyone’s problems she doesn’t want Eddie’s help.<br /><br />Throw in a Dolly Parton look-alike, a gruff but lovable strip club owner, Jet’s ne’er do well father, his ne’er do well friend, Bear, Bear’s long-suffering, chain-smoking wife Lavonne and the crew from Rock Chick and you’ve got Rock Chick Rescue.<br /><br />Rock Chick Rescue takes you on a wild ride with Jet, Eddie and the gang as they wrestle bad guys in a bagel shop, hit Denver’s backstreet poker tables (with big hair), and help the strippers at Smithie’s take down a would-be murderer.<br /><br />Through this, Jet’s got to learn that even when life made you give up your dreams, you can still end up with the (hot) guy. Eddie’s got to rescue Jet from a bad man (so he can do better things with her) and teach her that some dreams can come true.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1277082026367982212"><b>4 STARS</b><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>Confession time: I tried the first book of this series a few years ago and I didn’t care for it. Yep, sad but true. Years later and I’m running out of KA books and I have found myself in the middle of a full blown series binge read!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“It was like the Justice League of Super Heroes but instead it was the Justice League of Hot Guys.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>The cast of characters have grown on me in this second book. The heroine in this book, Jet McAllister is a wonderful daughter, employee and frie</span>
  <span id="freeText1277082026367982212" style="display:none"><b>4 STARS</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Confession time: I tried the first book of this series a few years ago and I didn’t care for it. Yep, sad but true. Years later and I’m running out of KA books and I have found myself in the middle of a full blown series binge read!<br><br><b>
  <i>“It was like the Justice League of Super Heroes but instead it was the Justice League of Hot Guys.” </i>
</b><br><br>The cast of characters have grown on me in this second book. The heroine in this book, Jet McAllister is a wonderful daughter, employee and friend. However, she SUCKED at being a girlfriend/lover. Her communication skills (ex. Pardon?) were horrendous and this girl ran every chance she had. <br><br>This is for Eddie… <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492367142ra/22510015.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I adored Eddie Chavez! He was the perfect KA hero for me. He’s not too pushy, he’s sexy as hell, and hit that something special mark where he felt like he was a living and breathing person for me. <br><br><b>
  <i>”I could fall in love with that smile,” he murmured as if he was talking to himself and I wasn’t even there.”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492367142ra/22510016.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jet’s father brings a ton of drama and danger to her doorstep and this independent woman must learn to truly accept help from others. Jet tried my patience and even though I could totally be friends with her, for a man like Eddie she missed the bar as his equal.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>Side Note: How cute is that Tex?<br><br><b>
  <i>”Don’t want you and your sister playin’ snotty tricks on me like those brats on TV,” Tex said. I blinked. “The brats on TV are usually kids, not adults approaching thirty like Lottie and me.”</i>
</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>”You like cats?”</i>
</b><br><br>I just can’t bring myself to rate this book lower than a 4 Star rating because of all the wonderful characters and one Eddie Chavez! <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1277082026367982212" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-kristen-ashley">author-kristen-ashley</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=reviewed-by-me">reviewed-by-me</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer299392553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14209033954292761487"><b>Re-read / Audio listen March 15th, 2015: </b><br/><br/>I'm totally loving my reread of the series, and I'm glad I decided to give the audio versions a try. The narrator, Susannah Jones, does a great job bringing the Rock Chicks, the Hot Bunch, and their stories to life!!<br/><br/><i>
  <b>This</b>
</i> is why I love Eddie: <br/><br/><i>“Whatever your next disaster, I’m gonna be there. Buying your groceries, fixin’ your car, dealin’ with your Dad, I don’t give a fuck. I want you to owe me. It gives me the upper hand, and I’m gonna need the upper </i></span>
  <span id="freeText14209033954292761487" style="display:none"><b>Re-read / Audio listen March 15th, 2015: </b><br /><br />I'm totally loving my reread of the series, and I'm glad I decided to give the audio versions a try. The narrator, Susannah Jones, does a great job bringing the Rock Chicks, the Hot Bunch, and their stories to life!!<br /><br /><i>
  <b>This</b>
</i> is why I love Eddie: <br /><br /><i>“Whatever your next disaster, I’m gonna be there. Buying your groceries, fixin’ your car, dealin’ with your Dad, I don’t give a fuck. I want you to owe me. It gives me the upper hand, and I’m gonna need the upper hand to wear you down. And Jet…”<br /><br /> He stopped, he was looking into my eyes , and he had that look he had this morning, after Mom and Lavonne came home and before I walked out of my room. The look made my belly feel funny and my knees get weak.<br /><br /> “What?” I asked. Honestly the suspense was killing me. <br /><br />“There’s one thing today proved.” He moved in even closer, his body was brushing mine and his face was an inch away.<br /><br /> “What? ” I kind of shouted. What could I say? It’d been a rough day. I was close to losing it. <br /><br />“Whatever happens, you’re worth it and I don’t want to hear you say again that you’re not. Get me?”<br /><br /> I felt that warm strangeness hit me and I had no choice but to nod. </i><br /><br /><b>Re-read Review - August 22-23, 2013</b><br /><br />Very few authors can tell a story that has me so caught up that I'm reading every word without skipping a single one, but Kristen Ashley can! And a re-read? Without skipping or skimming?? Nearly unheard of for me! But that's exactly what happened!<br /><br />Again, I was giggling my butt off, loving the chance to revisit some of the most amazing women ever - and the Hot Bunch, of course. What I loved most about this book was spending time with Tex and Daisy, two totally amazing people. Secondary characters? They sure as hell don't feel secondary. None of them do! They're ALL fantastic people I've come to adore. This book made me laugh, it made me smile, it had me fanning myself... Such a fun, feel-good story!<br /><br /><b>Original Review - </b><br /><br />Jet McAlister has spent most of her life solving everyone else’s <br />problems, handling all the hard stuff, taking care of the people she loves who just can’t seem to take care of themselves… and she’s done this even when it meant not taking care of <i>her</i>self. Working as a waitress in a strip club for the extra money to cover her mother’s medical expenses didn’t phase Jet at all, it was just another paycheck to help her help others. But one night after work when she ends up with a knife at her throat in the alley behind the club, wielded by someone looking for her family abandoning, sad excuse for a father, Jet’s friends aren’t about to let her ‘handle’ it herself. Whether she likes it or not, Jet has to answer to her Rock Chick friends and their men… and most definitely to Eddie Chavez who’s had the hots for Jet since the first time he laid eyes on her.<br /><br /><i>Rock Chick Rescue</i> is the second book in the <i>Rock Chick</i> series and seriously… laugh out loud funny, heart pounding exciting, and break out the fan and ice-water hot. I love, love, LOVE, the entire cast of characters and all the mischief and mayhem they manage to get into even when they’re just sitting around drinking coffee. <br /><br />If you haven’t yet tried Kristen Ashley’s writing and are wondering where to start, I strongly recommend the <i>Rock Chick </i>series. The heroes are hot and so alpha they make cavemen look like peace activists, and the women… they are funny as all get out, and sometimes it takes them awhile to “clue in,” but they are, in my opinion never, ever too stupid to live.<br /><br />I am soooooooo looking forward to the next book, and the one after that, and the one after that… I hope this author never stops writing Rock Chick stories.<br /><br />-----<br />If you're a Kristen Ashley addict, or just interested in checking her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492-kristen-ashley-addict-s-support-group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads! </span>
  <a data-text-id="14209033954292761487" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_497290167" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/497290167" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/497290167?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer497290167" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16007177828504071475"><b>4 Stars!!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/156ae7eb-f292-4df4-8fe6-69147050d577_zps666ecbe8.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403814i/785723.jpg' alt=' photo 156ae7eb-f292-4df4-8fe6-69147050d577_zps666ecbe8.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Jet McAlister is one of those girls that does everything for everyone. She is strong. She has no choice but to be strong. What would happen if she wasn’t? Everything would crumble. Her father is only in the picture when it’s convenient for him, her mother is recovering from a stroke, and her sister is in LA living big all the while Jet is working two jobs- coffee shop/bookstore by day and waitressing at a strip club at night. <br/><br/>Jet notices Eddie Chavez right away. He comes into Indy</span>
  <span id="freeText16007177828504071475" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars!!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/156ae7eb-f292-4df4-8fe6-69147050d577_zps666ecbe8.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403814i/785723.jpg" alt=" photo 156ae7eb-f292-4df4-8fe6-69147050d577_zps666ecbe8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jet McAlister is one of those girls that does everything for everyone. She is strong. She has no choice but to be strong. What would happen if she wasn’t? Everything would crumble. Her father is only in the picture when it’s convenient for him, her mother is recovering from a stroke, and her sister is in LA living big all the while Jet is working two jobs- coffee shop/bookstore by day and waitressing at a strip club at night. <br><br>Jet notices Eddie Chavez right away. He comes into Indy’s coffee shop often. Jet has a huge crush on Eddie. He is just her type, but she is extremely awkward around him. Eddie has a thing for Jet as well. Jet doesn’t have the highest self esteem/self worth. She doesn’t believe there is any way in the world Eddie could really want a girl like her. Shes ‘boring’. When Jet’s dad comes into town with a whole ton of trouble surrounding him, Jet proves to be anything BUT boring. <br><br>Jet and Eddie grow closer, but Jet feels Eddie is just there to rescue her, and once all her problems are gone, he will be too. She just doesn’t get it. Eddie has a job ahead of him. To prove to Jet that he will be what she needs, catch her when she falls, that she is worth it.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“Everyone's got their hands out waitin' for you to take one. You gotta learn when to take someone's hand before you fall.”</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/875e99e0-57f8-40f6-b3f8-cfc57afbede9_zps1696ffea.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403814i/785724.jpg" alt=" photo 875e99e0-57f8-40f6-b3f8-cfc57afbede9_zps1696ffea.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Jet and Eddie... Thank God for Eddie. All alpha male. All hot and sexy, protective, sweet and fine! Eddie and Jet balanced each other out. Although I liked Jet at times, and I understood her some of the time (being the older sibling, responsible one of the family) she really drove me insane for much of the book. She was the reason this wasn’t a 5 star read for me. I think if she would have came around a little earlier it wouldn’t have been as bad, but until the very last chapter she was working my nerves. Eddie was amazing. He really stuck it out there. He knew he had a good woman and he was willing to do whatever he had to do to keep her. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Chiquita, women spend a lot of time sittin’ around bitchin’ that there are no good men out there.<br>I hate to tell you this, but there aren’t a lot of good women either.<br>The difference is, when a man sees one, he knows it.<br>Then, he goes after her and wears her down until she’s his.<br>Then, if he’s any man at all, he won’t let her go.” </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br>I especially loved the scenes where Eddie worked on keeping Jet ‘sweet’. <br><br>For once in her life, Jet found someone to lean on. Some one she cares for, loves, and that makes her feel safe. Will she be able to let go of the feelings she harbors for herself and what she thinks she deserves and open up to Eddie... that is the question. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/be22eb51-5bfa-4281-83d7-a139cf1318ea_zps955ce4e0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380403814i/785725.jpg" alt=" photo be22eb51-5bfa-4281-83d7-a139cf1318ea_zps955ce4e0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> This had some suspense, action, it was frustrating at times, but it was also very funny. It was good to catch up with Indy, Tex, Duke, Ally, Lee and the whole gang...<br><b>
  <blockquote>It was like the Justice League of Super Heroes but instead it was the Justice League of Hot Guys.</blockquote>
</b> We also got to meet some fun new characters- Daisy, Ada, Smithie, Trixie etc. Love all of Lee’s guys and can’t wait to get to some of their books (especially Mace ♥) but next is Hank's book... bring it on! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16007177828504071475" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1762600989" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1762600989" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1762600989?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/11061689-rock-chick-rescue">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen">kristen-ashley-aka-the-queen</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1762600989" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10198286722886717204"><b> 4 stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Babe, watching you these past months has been like watching a flower bloom. Don't disappoint us.” ​</i> </b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474414297i/20596026._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>That horribly awkward moment where you identified with a character.... just to find out everyone who read the book hates her aka you.<br/><br/>I get ahead of myself. Rock Chick Rescue is the story of Jet and Eddie. We met them previously in the first book Rock Chick, where we learned Eddie was holding a torch for Indy and she chose Lee. Jet was more brief, but a quiet addition to the characters</span>
  <span id="freeText10198286722886717204" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Babe, watching you these past months has been like watching a flower bloom. Don't disappoint us.” ​</i> </b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1474414297i/20596026._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>That horribly awkward moment where you identified with a character.... just to find out everyone who read the book hates her aka you.<br><br>I get ahead of myself. Rock Chick Rescue is the story of Jet and Eddie. We met them previously in the first book Rock Chick, where we learned Eddie was holding a torch for Indy and she chose Lee. Jet was more brief, but a quiet addition to the characters near the end of the book.<br><br>Jet works two jobs to help support her mother who had a stroke less than a year ago. From the moment she laid eyes on Eddie she had a huge crush on him, but she just isn't able to talk to hot guys. When Jet's dad comes back into town bringing trouble into her life, Jet's secrets come out and Eddie and her coworkers and friends step up to help her out.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1456556813i/18248686.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> “Chiquita, women spend a lot of time sittin’ around bitchin’ that there are no good men out there.<br>I hate to tell you this, but there aren’t a lot of good women either.<br>The difference is, when a man sees one, he knows it.<br>Then, he goes after her and wears her down until she’s his.<br>Then, if he’s any man at all, he won’t let her go.” </i> </b><br><br>So like I said before, I actually really liked Jet. Maybe because I am often very insecure myself, I love when heroines aren't these strong and powerful women because I find "annoying" heroines refreshing and realistic. But that's just me. Hell I even liked Kiera from Thoughtless so judge me if you will.<br><br>Anyways, I normally don't enjoy Cinderella stories, but I really enjoyed this one. Mostly because Jet didn't lie down and expect Eddie to do everything for her, she really was self sufficient and worked hard for everything that came her way. Eddie was amazing, he's one of the better KA alpha heroes because he helped out Jet but he also gave her room to help herself.<br><br>One criticism..... this book constantly referred to Jet's lady parts as her "doo-da" and I had to put the book down when reading it because I can't even with that name. It was so awful.<br><br>This book just like the first also had me literally chuckling and laughing out loud while reading it. I think it's probably the funniest of Ashley's series and I cannot wait to read more as my book friends have said they get better and better as it goes on.<br><br><b> <i> “Everyone's got their hands out waitin' for you to take one. You gotta learn when to take someone's hand before you fall.” </i> </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1455783307i/18148833._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10198286722886717204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4778272948749665137"><b>2 stars</b><br/><br/>I will admit to mostly skimming this book. I wanted a basic understanding of the overall plot and to meet the new characters introduced in this story. I knew the heroine would drive me nuts, and from the little I read, I was correct. Luckily, I enjoyed Jet's character throughout the rest of the series. She was a pretty awesome character outside her own book. <br/><br/><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group' rel='nofollow noopener'>Kristen Ashley Addict's S</a></i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2676399739383976350"><b>★Book Basics★</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Cont. Romance<br/><b>
  <i>Series</i>
</b>: - 2nd in the series<br/><b>
  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Cheating?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>HEA? -</i>
</b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Would I read more by this author/or in this series? </i>

  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 5<br /><br /><br /><b>★Review★</b><br /><br />Reviewing after what must be my 15th re read of this book. <br /><br />Shall keep it short.<br /><br />LOVE LOVE LOVE Eddie. Adored Jet, even if she drove me insane at times. <br /><br />I enjoyed how Jet had spent most of her life, looking out for others, sacrificing for her family, yet in this book she has an entire group of people all stood there willing to be her back up and catch her when she falls. With Eddie right at the front of that group.<br /><br />Eddie had spent months trying to get Jet's attention, and when he eventually has his chance, he refuses to let anything, even Jet herself, spoil it. <br /><br />Add in some bad guys, a bit of drama, some funny moments, and it is an excellent 5 stars.<br /><br />A great addition to the Rock Chick series, and one of my favourite couples in the series - shall be a book I re read many more times.</span>

<div id="review_344635263" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/344635263" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/344635263?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer344635263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9125297036868924130">I gotta say I did like this book, but I didn’t love it nearly as much as the first one.<br/><br/>Jet meets Eddie when she gets a job working at the coffee shop run by Indy (the heroine from book 1). Jet is trying her best to get by working two jobs while taking care of her mother who has suffered from a stroke. Eddie is a cop who works with Lee Nightingale (the insanely HOT hero from book 1). They have nearly instant mutual attraction but while Eddie tries his best to act on it, Jet tries her best to defl</span>
  <span id="freeText9125297036868924130" style="display:none">I gotta say I did like this book, but I didn’t love it nearly as much as the first one.<br><br>Jet meets Eddie when she gets a job working at the coffee shop run by Indy (the heroine from book 1). Jet is trying her best to get by working two jobs while taking care of her mother who has suffered from a stroke. Eddie is a cop who works with Lee Nightingale (the insanely HOT hero from book 1). They have nearly instant mutual attraction but while Eddie tries his best to act on it, Jet tries her best to deflect his efforts. Then in walks her Dad who has gotten himself indebted to the wrong lone sharks who are willing to drag anyone into the mess and Jet ends up under Eddie’s protection as he makes it his business to keep her safe.<br><br>Eddie was an awesome hero. He was HOT, possessive, protective, patient, caring and everything a hero should be – I absolutely loved him!! But Jet really brought the book down for me – she literally had no sense of self worth and her constant insistence right until the last page of the book that she didn’t deserve Eddie/they weren’t right for each other really frustrated me. I understand where she was coming from – her Dad abandoned her Mom when she was a kid so her faith in men was sorely shaken, but I still wished there would have been a point where she came around so we could actually see more of them as a functional couple. <br><br>Eddie worked so hard to make them work as a couple (and in the end won of course) but I kinda wished that Jet would have tried a little harder too.<br><br><b> <i> “Eddie, let me go!” I (kind of) shouted.<br>His arms tightened and he shook me a bit. “It’s not gonna happen!” he shouted back. </i> </b><br><br>As usual with all KA books, we have a wonderful mix of action and romance. And I absolutely LOVED that all the characters from book 1 that we have come to know and love not only showed up in this book, but were integral parts of the story. Also, I loved that the stories of the past couples continue in this book, they don’t just become side characters, its absolutely wonderful to see them moving on with their lives together.<br><br><i> “Let me guess, this one has your protection too? What? Are you building a harem?” </i><br><br>KA is an absolute genius at building a complex network of relationships and friendships that just make me squee! There is a scene at the end where literally everyone works together and it gave me shivers!!<br><br><i> “Holy crap,” I whispered. <br>It was like the Justice League of Super Heroes but instead it was the Justice League of Hot Guys.” </i><br><br>Also, with what I’ve seen of the other characters whose books are still to come, I know I absolutely cannot WAIT for their stories and I have heard that their heroines are not annoying so yay!! Mace in particular I have fallen in love with! He’s tortured and dark and broody and HOT *swooon* … must. read. faster. lol<br><br>Here’s how I see Eddie and Jet:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380380175i/736948._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9125297036868924130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13687553513039886991"><b> 4 "You're so full of sh*t" STARS</b><br/><br/>The adventure, hilarity and steamy sexy times continues for the Rock Chick gang with Jet McAllister and Eddie Chavez's story. <br/><br/>Jet was silly, cute and shy, although I could have done without her 'ekes' and 'sheeshes', and especially calling her vagina a "do-da". What are we, 10? Perhaps it was because this was an audiobook that her quirks seemed more prominent and if I'd read it, they might've been less annoying (I would've down played them in my head!). But don't</span>
  <span id="freeText13687553513039886991" style="display:none"><b> 4 "You're so full of sh*t" STARS</b><br /><br />The adventure, hilarity and steamy sexy times continues for the Rock Chick gang with Jet McAllister and Eddie Chavez's story. <br /><br />Jet was silly, cute and shy, although I could have done without her 'ekes' and 'sheeshes', and especially calling her vagina a "do-da". What are we, 10? Perhaps it was because this was an audiobook that her quirks seemed more prominent and if I'd read it, they might've been less annoying (I would've down played them in my head!). But don't get me wrong, Susannah Jones does an awesome job on the audio. <br /><br />And Eddie, melt my panties!! He was all kinds of alpha and I loved how into Jet he was even though he played it cool. Because seriously, for what that chick put him through, he had to be wild about her or absolutely insane! LOL. And his moments of sweet were classic KA, had me swooning and my belly doing a pitter-patter!<br /><br /><b>“I could fall in love with that smile”</b><br /><br />Onto the next one book. Rock on!<br /><br /><br /></span>

    <a title="bella farren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23223005-bella-farren"><img alt="bella farren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598064440p2/23223005.jpg" /></a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/23223005-bella-farren?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1950013442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11484423191879027205"><b>4/5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>reread:</b> <br/>14/05/18<br/>02/06/19 <br/><br/><s>Another good addition to the <i>Rock Chick</i> series but nothing overly spectacular. I enjoyed Eddie's character and the drama that unfolded throughout the book, with stabbings and characters nearly having their heads shot off but the romance between Jet and Eddie was a little meh, not my favourite. </s><br/><br/><b>AHEM. Clearly 2017 Bella was out of her ever loving mind. I love Eddie and although Jet was sometimes (often) frustrating and annoying, I still adore them. Bumping this up</b></span>
  <span id="freeText11484423191879027205" style="display:none"><b>4/5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>reread:</b> <br />14/05/18<br />02/06/19 <br /><br /><s>Another good addition to the <i>Rock Chick</i> series but nothing overly spectacular. I enjoyed Eddie's character and the drama that unfolded throughout the book, with stabbings and characters nearly having their heads shot off but the romance between Jet and Eddie was a little meh, not my favourite. </s><br /><br /><b>AHEM. Clearly 2017 Bella was out of her ever loving mind. I love Eddie and although Jet was sometimes (often) frustrating and annoying, I still adore them. Bumping this up to the 4 stars it deserves. </b> I think when you read this series in order, you appreciate the characters and their stories a lot more. The second book will never shape up next to the sixth when hundreds more crazy characters and relationships join in; you need the lead up and anticipation. (My hypothesis to why 2017 Bella didn't appreciate this gem lol). <br /><br />I still enjoyed the story and seeing more of my beloved characters. I found that I enjoyed Jet more as a side character in the later novels rather than as a main character, I found that she tended to get on my nerves in such big doses. Jet is a female character who 'supposedly' doesn't see herself as everybody else does, she thinks she is boring in ever department and Eddie is forced to make her see herself in the same light he does. It's a familiar trope and one that tends to start to irritate me, especially when the character in question makes stupid decisions because of it—aka Jet. <br /><br />Not my favourite but still an enjoyable addition that I'm sure I'll go back and reread when I need a good dose of romance. <br /><br /><b>my reviews and ratings for <i>Kristen Ashely's</i> other books:</b><br />• <a <span id="freeTextContainer3285396376428357983">3 ½ stars – Chick lit/Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br/><br/>Geez, and here I thought Indy from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_' title='Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rock Chick</a> was aggravating.   <span id="freeText3285396376428357983" style="display:none">3 ½ stars – Chick lit/Contemporary Romance/Romantic Suspense<br /><br />Geez, and here I thought Indy from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_" title="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a> was aggravating. But Jet definitely wins the prize for the most annoying, clueless, low self-esteem, and TSTL heroine who’s deserving of a major b*tch slap smackdown. I found her so exasperating that she lessened my overall enjoyment, and I don’t know why a yummy as sin hero like Eddie put up with all her bullsh*t, unless he’s just glutton for punishment. <br /><br />But it’s still Kristen Ashley, so of course, despite my loathing Jet, the wacky, unbelievable plot, zany antics, and super abrupt ending, I still found it entertaining. And I’ll definitely read the rest of the <i>Rock Chick</i> series.<br /><br />*****Edited from original rating/review*****<br /><br />I bumped this from a low 3.5 to a higher 3.5 (closer to 4 stars) after finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13184992.Rock_Chick_Regret__Rock_Chick___7_" title="Rock Chick Regret (Rock Chick, #7) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick Regret</a>, <i>loving</i> the series, and eventually growing to like Jet!<br /><br /></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1772108601" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2762982390044061503">I want to make glass thingies of the word <i>eek</i> -if we can call it a word-. And then smash them all into little eeky pieces with a baseball bat. I want dead little <i>eek</i>s littering the ground. There were around a hundred too many of eeks in this boring book about an annoying twat who thought that her hair/her room/her looks/her life/her fucking everything is boring. And you know what? She was damn right! This "bohhuuu pity my boringness" kept going on till the last page and was practically the what </span>
  <span id="freeText2762982390044061503" style="display:none">I want to make glass thingies of the word <i>eek</i> -if we can call it a word-. And then smash them all into little eeky pieces with a baseball bat. I want dead little <i>eek</i>s littering the ground. There were around a hundred too many of eeks in this boring book about an annoying twat who thought that her hair/her room/her looks/her life/her fucking everything is boring. And you know what? She was damn right! This "bohhuuu pity my boringness" kept going on till the last page and was practically the what the whole book was about. I kept picturing myself running circles around the heroine chanting <i>boring boring boring</i> and sprinkling crazy screams of <i>eek</i> wordies in between my spit riddled crazy dance of violence. Hmm, it looked better in my head. Nevermind!<br /><br /><br />Another word Jet loves is <i>doo-da</i> in reference to her vagina or clit, I'm not sure which one exactly. This being the first time I've seen it, I went and asked uncle google what it means. These are some of the results;<br /><br />1-Grandfather figure...<br />often gruff but also very kind and loyal.<br /><br />2-Rear end, bottom butt<br /><br />3-The name of a curious clown woman you might find snooping around Mcdonalds after the sun sets. She usually appears in her clown form and may quite possibly be drunk off her ass. Young men should stay far from her, for she has little manners and may invite them and their cocks into her massive clown puss. Basically, a Doo-Da is a <u>clown whore</u>.<br /><br />As you can guess I'm gonna go with the third explanation because when I think of the whole book that's the one that makes sense.<br /><br /><br />I just wanted to knock <s>hard</s> lightly on Jet's -who is our main <s>twat</s> heroine- head and ask; is there anybody home?! Say you're minding your business and drinking your espresso. A man you like comes and swipes his thumb trough your lip, then sucks the said thumb. What would you think? I'll tell you what Jet thinks; "he does this because he is being nice to me". Yeah, that's the logical answer, you go girl!!<br /><br /><br />At some point Jet says; <i>I was such an idiot. No I was beyond idiot, though I didn’t know what beyond idiot was.</i> Let momma Bubs tell you what's beyond the idiot my little Jetty; being an idiotic pipsqueak fucktard -like you. Even bitching about Jet is boring so I'll get to our hero; Eddie.<br /><br /><br />Eddie is ... just there... doing stuff, going about his <s>pussy</s> puppy love trying to look like an alpha. Trying is good but doesn't guarantee success. He says "<i>If you’re indebted to me, you’re connected to me.</i>" to explain how he is going to keep his relationship with Jet. I don't have much to say about him other than I think he needs to go see a shrink about what he finds "adorable" in a woman and his ideas about healthy relationships.<br /><br /><br />Other characters were ok. I'm intrigued by Mace and Lottie so I'll probably read more of this series in the future when I feel the need to rant, but for now we have to part ways with this author before I go into homicidal rage.</span>

I think I'm even okay that they are open 7 days a week. I'm talking no time for friends, guys or a life whatsoever. Then dear ole daddy brings trouble to her doorstep and she is forced into a life she never expected. When knifes started being flashed and bullets start flying Eddie steps in and claims what he has wanted for months. All of a sudden Jet is kidnapped, threatened to be hunted down and told graphically how she is going to be raped. Wanting life to go back to normal Jet goes against what Eddie tells her to do and from Rock Chick gang member to the next finds herself in different situations. (May I just say, Lee has his hands full with Indy, seeing as how she is sometimes the instigator but always always on a ride along in the craziness.)<br><br><b> "I think you best mosey on up ther, pa'dner. Trixie, Ada, Nancy, Lottie, Blanca and the rest of Eddie's family was just all awesome additions. <br><br>I just really feel like I'm rambling, so I'll say this is an awesome KA series full of macho alpha men, suspense, hilarious Rock Chicks who get themselves in trouble more than not, and love in the end. Highly recommended if you haven't read it. Can't wait for more. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16605518267601608493"><i>Written July 8, 2014</i><br/><br/><b>3.8 Stars - “Eak” good<br/><br/>Book #2 </b><br/><br/>I got this one (and the rest of them..) as an (new) audiobook for a nice price <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ ($2 or just $6 + a kindlebook)  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. ~ I've heard plenty good things about the 'chick'-books so it felt like <b>a great decision to take the time and listening them this summer.</b>.<br/><br/>I liked the first one <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546672664' rel='nofollow noopener'>#1 -Rock Chick (3.5 stars)</a> about Indy & Lee. It was a joy to listening to that one, so this second part could just be better if I understand all m</span>
  <span id="freeText16605518267601608493" style="display:none"><i>Written July 8, 2014</i><br><br><b>3.8 Stars - “Eak” good<br><br>Book #2 </b><br><br>I got this one (and the rest of them..) as an (new) audiobook for a nice price <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ ($2 or just $6 + a kindlebook)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. ~ I've heard plenty good things about the 'chick'-books so it felt like <b>a great decision to take the time and listening them this summer.</b>.<br><br>I liked the first one <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/546672664" rel="nofollow noopener">#1 -Rock Chick (3.5 stars)</a> about Indy &amp; Lee. It was a joy to listening to that one, so this second part could just be better if I understand all my friends right. <br><br><a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://yoursmiles.org/m-girls.php?page=3" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1403647828ra/10124281.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>...14 audio hours later in this crazy 'chick world': Ones more nicely narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/8109353.Susannah_Jones" title="Susannah Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">Susannah Jones</a>. It was a tiny bit better story in <i> RC Rescue</i> than the first one. Less chatter and more focus. Superb fun, hot and sooo romantic.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br>This time we meet <b>Eddie Chavez</b> (Lee's best friend and the <i>swoo-gorgeous-latino</i> we remember from #1) and <b>Jet McAlister</b> a new employee in Indy's bookshop. <br><br>Jet is a very very stressed girl. She takes care of her sick mother and work all the time. Also, she is the kind of beautiful girl who never has seen herself in a mirror and can't understand why a boyfriend's dream like Eddie is interest in a "plain-dull-and-simple" girl like herself. It surely can not be serious, right?<br><blockquote>“Everyone's got their hands out waitin' for you to take one. You gotta learn when to take someone's hand before you fall.”<br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/Couple%20in%20love/?action=view&amp;current=31d3ea07387114587e927afbbb14ed71_zps3ffe1c0e.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404676514i/10271417.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>It was a lot of moaning, sighing, smacking, whining, laughing, crying</b> and of course memorable male hero statements, even in this one. But I like all these cute and loved KA attributes. ~ <i>Eak!!</i><br><br>Jet, her mother and her mother's female friends were completely gorgeous. Eddie did not appear quite as flirty charming this time ... but my god what an attractive <b>M</b>an (with a big fat M) he is. Which healthy woman wouldn't want to drown in his dark (hot) latino eyes? I stand in the queue...<br><blockquote>“Chiquita, women spend a lot of time sittin’ around bitchin’ that there are no good men out there.<br>I hate to tell you this, but there aren’t a lot of good women either. The difference is, when a man sees one, he knows it. Then, he goes after her and wears her down until she’s his. Then, if he’s any man at all, he won’t let her go.” <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/albums/w615/Li64/Wear/shoes/?action=view&amp;current=39ecfe870ed1d9eb6eb4aa0def7cacfc_zps4d4fc3b0.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1404677198i/10271522.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>This is easy and fun ear candy</b>, perfect for lazy days on the beach. ~ I'm lazy, it's summer, so there will be no more than this. <br><br>Looking forward to start listening to the third book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/968560947?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">#3 - Rock Chick Redemption</a> about <i>Hank Nightingale</i> and <i>Roxie</i>. Another 14 audio hours from this crazy fun 'chick' world. <br><br><b>I LIKE - irresistible chicks and their men....Wow!!</b><br><br><br>*******<br><i> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380379176i/735273.jpg" width="80" height="70" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> The <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69392-rock-chick" rel="nofollow noopener">Rock Chick</a> series by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2958084.Kristen_Ashley" title="Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley</a> </i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6538757.Rock_Chick__Rock_Chick___1_" title="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1266750153s/6538757.jpg" alt="Rock Chick (Rock Chick, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7405450.Rock_Chick_Rescue__Rock_Chick___2_" title="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1416398897s/7405450.jpg" alt="Rock Chick Rescue (Rock Chick, #2) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_263365229" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/263365229" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/263365229?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer263365229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2077869961736720101">Aaaand, we're back to why I love KA so much. Though Ms. Ashley strayed a bit from her usual heroine with Jet, there was still so much to love about her. Since she was fourteen, she's taken care of everyone but herself. She's basically supported her mom and sister emotionally and monetarily since her dad took off. Now, her sister lives in California and her Mom had a stroke. Jet moves in with her mom to once again take care of her, and is working herself to exhaustion day and night just to try to</span>
  <span id="freeText2077869961736720101" style="display:none">Aaaand, we're back to why I love KA so much. Though Ms. Ashley strayed a bit from her usual heroine with Jet, there was still so much to love about her. Since she was fourteen, she's taken care of everyone but herself. She's basically supported her mom and sister emotionally and monetarily since her dad took off. Now, her sister lives in California and her Mom had a stroke. Jet moves in with her mom to once again take care of her, and is working herself to exhaustion day and night just to try to get by. She doesn't have a single second to spare, especially for someone like Eddie, who seems to take up a lot of her time just thinking about him.<br /><br />Who could take a name like Eddie and make it sound sexy? This author can! Gimme that sexy Spanish accent calling me (okay, Jet) <i>carina</i> and I'm a melty puddle of goo, right next to Jet on the floor. <br /><br />"He has a lean body made up of compact, defined muscles and he's one of those guys who makes whatever he wears look the bomb, instead of one of those guys who looks like he was trying to be the bomb in what he wears."<br /><br />Mmmmhmmm, I know what you're saying. I fell in love with both Jet and Eddie from page eight, when she starts listing off their first encounters and her subsequent bouts of stupidity in the face of Eddie's hotness. But you can tell the whole time that each time Jet slips up, Eddie falls harder for her. For nearly the entire book, she just can't understand what a guy like Eddie is doing with a girl like her. In fact, Eddie even says, multiple times, "You just don't <i>see</i> it, do you?" And my GOODNESS, can this man talk! <br /><br />"Since I'm being honest with you, Chiquita, I'll tell you that I usually play with what I want until I feel the time is right to move in. The time was right with you a long fuckin' time ago but you've been so focused on your own shit, you gave me no opening. This hasn't been fast. You want to see fast, we'll go into the bedroom and I'll show you fast but I'll show it to you slow."<br /><br />Just a little taste of Eddie, there. One thing that I noticed about this series so far is that the plain talking so prevalent in the Colorado Mountain series is still there, but waaay toned down. It's not hard to read the male dialogue. And KA doesn't use a dictionary/thesaurus to write. I think that's why its so easy to connect with her characters. You could be talking to your (really hot) neighbor or (sexy as hell) friend's brother. <br /><br />Of course, Tex and the gang from Fortnums is back, as well as the studly crew of law enforcement and secretive gang of hotness. I can tell already that Mace is going to be one of my flavorite boys. There is a scene in here with Mace that breaks my heart and heats me up, all at the same time. I'm telling you, in the middle of my Eddie worship, I wanted to stop and just skip to Mace's story. Really. PLEASE tell me Mace gets a story. Please. I'm done now, and where I usually take a break after two series books in a row, I don't think its possible with this series. I'm smitten, by all of the men in this series. Each is so different, yet still retain that uber-possessive alpha streak that grabs ahold of me. Yummy, yumm! <b>I am so freakin' stoked to get to the rest of this series!</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2077869961736720101" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1488176455" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1488176455" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1488176455?book_show_action=true">Dec 31, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1488176455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16233443175026923547"><b>Sale Alert:</b> Kindle Deal 29Nov19 for <a href='' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.99</a><br/><br/><b>2.5 OMG I Can't Believe I Rated a KA book so low Stars.</b><br/><br/>Read with my fellow KA Woo-Girls at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br/><br/>It was bound to happen….eventually <i>*takes a deep breath*</i> I didn’t like Eddie and Jet. *Whew* there I said it and I’m still standing. Okay so they are my least favorite couple out of all the KA-land couples. It’s really okay because they have some very stiff competition but something was missing in this story for me. Some of the stuff that ne</span>
  <span id="freeText16233443175026923547" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert:</b> Kindle Deal 29Nov19 for <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99</a><br /><br /><b>2.5 OMG I Can't Believe I Rated a KA book so low Stars.</b><br /><br />Read with my fellow KA Woo-Girls at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br /><br />It was bound to happen….eventually <i>*takes a deep breath*</i> I didn’t like Eddie and Jet. *Whew* there I said it and I’m still standing. Okay so they are my least favorite couple out of all the KA-land couples. It’s really okay because they have some very stiff competition but something was missing in this story for me. Some of the stuff that never bugs me in a KA story totally bothered me here. Good thing that there are still so many great side characters and fun things happening that even though I didn’t absolutely love the main couple I still had a pretty decent time.<br /><br /><b>The Good:</b><br /><br />♥ - Seeing Indy and Lee and all the gang from the previous book. I love them all and they were so much fun in this one too. I can’t even decide who I liked the most. Indy….Lee….Mace *cries for Mace*…Daisy or Tex. It is probably Tex. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m comin’ too,” he announced. <br />I closed my eyes. This was spiraling out-of-control. I opened them again. “Please listen to me—” <br />“No way, Loopy Loo. You aren’t hoardin’ all the action.” He turned to Indy, “You’re drivin’ because we can all fit in your silly-ass car. When we see a break in the coffee action, I’ll go home and get my shotgun.” <br />My mouth dropped open and I was pretty sure my eyes bugged out of my head. <br />“Don’t worry, Jet. Just as long as we don’t get into any situations that require grenades, we’ll be fine.” Indy said this like she wasn’t joking.<br /> Tex looked at Indy for a beat. “I’ll pack a few, just in case,” he said</i>
</blockquote><br />Seriously I love that dude and he could be my unofficial body guard any day. Also seeing him flustered by someone he was interested in was fantastic and adorable.<br /><br />But Daisy comes in a close second. She looks a little bit like a younger Dolly Parton and she is just a hoot and a holler ya’ll. She is also married to a very dangerous man but she is so easy to love right from the beginning. I loved all her costumes and sparkles.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“What’s happening?” I asked. <br />“Daisy’s going to take me to Smithie’s, show me some moves, make sure I get my Porsche,” Lottie explained. “Mom’s gonna come with us.” <br />I thought about Mom hanging out at Smithie’s watching her daughter practice strip routines. <br />My family</i>
</blockquote> <br />♡ - The crazy mothers. Both Jet and Eddie have mothers who are all kinds of meddling. It’s cute how badly each of them wants their child to find a relationship, happiness and get to the place of giving them some grandbabies. What is even funnier is how they don’t even try to hide it.<br /><br />♥ - <b>Crazy kidnappings</b>….I know they can be sorta cheesy but I really love knowing that the heroine at some time or another in this series is going to be kidnapped and not always by someone really bad. Sometimes it is by someone who isn’t exactly on team Nightingale but is not exactly against team Nightingale either. Frenemies Lee and Eddie have them.<br /><br />♡ - Just the fun banter and familiarity with the entire group. Daisy was so much but so are Tod, Ally, Indy and even Hank in his uber gruff manner. They all add that small hometownfeel to the story and I totally love how KA does this probably better than most.<br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I do not worship at the altar of Sarah Jessica Parker and all things Sex and the City to go out with a hot-lookin’ girlie in black flats. <b>You wear black flats when you’re eight and ninety-eight, not anytime in between.”</b> <br />“Tod—” <br />“Huh!” he snapped, giving me The Hand. I knew better than to argue with The Hand. So, if something went down and I couldn’t run, at least I’d die dressed to the nines from top-to-toe.</i>
</blockquote><br /><b>The Bad</b><br /><br />Look some of the story didn’t make a ton of sense. Jet is taking care of her mother who had a stroke and is running herself ragged doing everything by herself. But it comes out later that there were people who could have helped her and she just didn’t let anyone know….including her sister. It is the sister part I didn’t get, it seemed so natural that her sister would help in some way. But *shrugs* that would have detracted from Jet being a martyr and worth getting her own Alpha man.<br /><br />Okay in the beginning I was really pulling for Jet. She is doing so much for her mom and has stretched herself so thin and she has this totally low self-esteem. I connected with her really well in the beginning but Jet never got out of the mindset that she deserved to have anyone in her life and she was always just seconds away from dropping Eddie and never seeing him again. Even at the end there didn’t seem to be any solidification of the couple they became. It was weird and while bravo to KA for doing something different in her story and not having the couple really tight but at the same time I missed that sort of ending.<br /><br /><b>I didn’t love the lingo in this one</b> there weren’t any super adorable nicknames and for some reason the Spanish just didn’t work for me. Plus Jet called her lady parts a doo dah and every time she did that the sexiness of the moment just left me.<br /><br />Eddie was pretty okay for me as an alpha male went. He did pretty well with Jet considering she was always trying to kick him out of her life and do everything by herself. Like I said the Spanish endearments didn’t really work for me but almost everything else about Eddie did until something near the very end, but it wasn’t a deal breaker or anything like that, just some alpha macho madness. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>I already told you that you were my business, but it’s pretty fuckin’ clear you didn’t understand. I’ve been tryin’ to get your attention for months, but you’re so busy and exhausted and whatever the hell else you are it hasn’t worked. So I’ll say, straight out, so there’s no confusion. I want to spend time with you, I want to get to know you, and I want to sleep with you and it doesn’t have to be in that order.”</i>
</blockquote><br /> I liked that Eddie understood Jet, he knew when she was getting scared and ready to bail and that worked for me. But the ending to this book didn’t really feel like an ending at all. It was totally abrupt and I feel like I didn’t get closure on their love story.<br /><br /><b>But Never Fear</b> - there were enough little snippets of the other Rock Chick men with hints of their stories to come that I’m just gonna keep on keeping on until I get through the entire series. <b>After this book I am the most interested in Mace’s upcoming book.</b> I can already tell that one will be an emotional rollercoaster and I can’t wait to go for my ride.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16233443175026923547" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1498509229" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1498509229" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1498509229?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jilly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jilly" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly">Jilly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=buddy-read-with-bbbs">buddy-read-with-bbbs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25894509-jilly?shelf=contemporary-fiction">contemporary-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1498509229" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9998808276890252769">The best parts of this book, for me, were when the characters from the first book were there. I absolutely love this gang of people and their crazy antics. Also, I think I want a stun gun.<br/><br/>Our couple in this book are Eddie, Lee's best friend and character from the last book who is also a cop, and Jet, a new girl working at the coffee counter in Indy's book store.<br/><br/>Eddie is a former playa, reformed bad-boy, and complete alpha male. As a matter of fact, he is waaaaay too much alpha male for me. I lik</span>
  <span id="freeText9998808276890252769" style="display:none">The best parts of this book, for me, were when the characters from the first book were there. I absolutely love this gang of people and their crazy antics. Also, I think I want a stun gun.<br><br>Our couple in this book are Eddie, Lee's best friend and character from the last book who is also a cop, and Jet, a new girl working at the coffee counter in Indy's book store.<br><br>Eddie is a former playa, reformed bad-boy, and complete alpha male. As a matter of fact, he is waaaaay too much alpha male for me. I like confidence and the ability to take charge, but when it comes to being pushed around by a guy? No.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452246455i/17665679._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Now tell me I can't hit the f*cking snooze button in the morning, Dickhead!</i><br><br>Jet, our narrator and heroine, is a beautiful girl ( but mysteriously doesn't know it) who takes care of her disabled mother by working two jobs. She's a total push-over and has a bit of a martyr complex if you ask me. Most people I know have had lives just as tough as hers, but they don't walk around like Eeyore all the time. Suck it up, buttercup!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452246455i/17665680.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Jet took the Buzzfeed Quiz: Which Disney Character are you? She knew she'd get someone bad. Her life sucks....</i><br><br>Jet's deadbeat, loser dad comes into town and immediately screws up Jet's already lousy life. She is now in danger from some bad guys who are trying to get to dear old dad, so Eddie takes over. He is a total steamroller, but that's okay because he's hot. Stalker-like behavior is totally cool if a guy is hot, don't ya know?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1452246455i/17665681._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i> in other words, they're dependable? I think I'm in love!!</i><br><br>There are some great moments, but most of those involve Indy, Ally, and Tex from the last book. On their own, I wasn't a huge fan of Eddie and Jet - I was a fan of their families, but not them so much. That's how these series work, some of the couples are great, some are so-so. I'm still happy with the series and will continue on.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9998808276890252769" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1862910808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1512671253412207156">OMG. I loved Eddie in Rock Chick and was so happy his story was up next! <br/><br/>Jet is working two jobs, taking care of everyone but herself when her dad rolls back into town and everything goes to shit. Eddie took notice of the shy beauty a while ago, but with trouble knocking on her door, he’s not taking a backseat to protecting her – even if she doesn’t willingly accept his help.<br/><br/>I loved the dynamic between these two. Even though Jet drove me crazy with her hot/cold routine, I loved Eddie pushing eve</span>
  <span id="freeText1512671253412207156" style="display:none">OMG. I loved Eddie in Rock Chick and was so happy his story was up next! <br /><br />Jet is working two jobs, taking care of everyone but herself when her dad rolls back into town and everything goes to shit. Eddie took notice of the shy beauty a while ago, but with trouble knocking on her door, he’s not taking a backseat to protecting her – even if she doesn’t willingly accept his help.<br /><br />I loved the dynamic between these two. Even though Jet drove me crazy with her hot/cold routine, I loved Eddie pushing every step of the way. I loved that he thought she was worth it. And the stun gun. The fucking stun gun. Again. So fucking hilarious. I am hoping shit happens in all the books, because I can’t get enough of it.<br /><br />I finished this book and all I can think about Mace. He stole my heart in one scene and although Hank is up next and I am sure I’ll love him. I sort of really want to read more about Mace. <br /></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('l/tSqmCIPDw9IpwP+idaBWNYQYqb6OxDmhg6a5rLtfRufOq1AIjoEpZBJPIjqeHVI325NY87l2gaFiF2HuDhqg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Xuduv4uFHUP3gE4rAIpxWVH82gT6sbexsmdP7KI5s1+nYNag64XJbVzj9tbZBMqJEdkiu+5izJoyaVTxJhLnAQ==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer4724884298327159846">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br/><br/>Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends a</span>
  <span id="freeText4724884298327159846" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
